class="entry-category"><a  href="https://www.euroweeklynews.com/quirky/">Quirky</a></li></ul>\r\n            <header class="td-post-title">\r\n                <h1 class="entry-title">Chemicals in cannabis are helping cure COVID-19</h1>\r\n                \r\n\r\n                <div class="td-module-meta-info">\r\n                    <!-- author --><div class="td-post-author-name"><div class="td-author-by">By</div> <a href="https://www.euroweeklynews.com/author/charlie-ewn/">Charlie Loran</a><div class="td-author-line"> - </div> </div>                    <!-- date --><span class="td-post-date"><time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2020-10-06T09:40:52+02:00" >6  October 2020 @ 09:40</time></span>                    <!-- comments --><div class="td-post-comments"><a href="https://www.euroweeklynews.com/2020/10/06/chemicals-in-cannabis-are-helping-cure-covid-19/#respond"><i class="td-icon-comments"></i>0</a></div>                    <!-- views -->                </div>\r\n\r\n            </header>\r\n\r\n        </div>\r\n\r\n        \r\n        <div class="td-post-content tagdiv-type">\r\n            <!-- image --><div class="td-post-featured-image"><figure><img width="523" height="278" class="entry-thumb lazy" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=\'http://www.w3.org/2000/svg\'%20viewBox=\'0%200%20523%20278\'%3E%3C/svg%3E" data-src="https://cdn.euroweeklynews.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Screenshot-2020-10-05-135154.jpg?x26592" data-srcset="https://cdn.euroweeklynews.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Screenshot-2020-10-05-135154.jpg?x26592 523w, https://cdn.euroweeklynews.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Screenshot-2020-10-05-135154-300x159.jpg?x26592 300w" data-sizes="(max-width: 523px) 100vw, 523px" alt="Chemicals in cannabis are helping cure COVID-19" title="Screenshot 2020-10-05 135154"/><figcaption class="wp-caption-text">Chemicals from cannabis are helping find a cure for COVID-19  Credit - Twitter</figcaption></figure></div>\r\n            <!-- content --><div class="at-above-post addthis_tool" data-url="https://www.euroweeklynews.com/2020/10/06/chemicals-in-cannabis-are-helping-cure-covid-19/"></div><p>CHEMICALS in cannabis are helping cure COVID-19, research has shown promising results in the treatment of serious complications caused by COVID-19.</p>\n<p><span id="more-221202"></span></p><div class="td-a-rec td-a-rec-id-content_inline  tdi_68_c66 td_block_template_14">\n<style>\n/* custom css */\n.tdi_68_c66.td-a-rec{\r\n\t\t\t\t\ttext-align: center;\r\n\t\t\t\t}.tdi_68_c66 .td-element-style{\r\n\t\t\t\t\tz-index: -1;\r\n\t\t\t\t}.tdi_68_c66.td-a-rec-img{\r\n\t\t\t\t    text-align: left;\r\n\t\t\t\t}.tdi_68_c66.td-a-rec-img img{\r\n                    margin: 0 auto 0 0;\r\n                }@media (max-width: 767px) {\r\n\t\t\t\t    .tdi_68_c66.td-a-rec-img {\r\n\t\t\t\t        text-align: center;\r\n\t\t\t\t    }\r\n                }\n</style><span class="td-adspot-title">-- Advertisement --</span><!-- Snack-Media INSIDE ADSS -->\r\n<div style="margin:10px auto 10px auto; text-align:center; width:100%; overflow:hidden;">\r\n\t<div id="snack_dex6"></div>\r\n</div>\r\n<br></div>\n<p>Scientists used THC \xe2\x80\x93 the main psychoactive compound found in marijuana, on mice suffering from Acute Respiratory Distress Syndrome (ARDS). The disease is a life-threatening condition when fluid builds up in the lungs, meaning they cannot provide the body with enough vital oxygen.</p>\n<p><a href="https://www.euroweeklynews.com/2020/01/16/health-news-scientists-uncover-key-information-that-could-help-fight-alzheimers/">It is one of the most common and serious complications brought on by COVID-19 and can be fatal.</a></p>\n<p>The University of South Carolina researchers wanted to see if THC, which has shown to act as a potent anti-inflammatory, could be effective at protecting mice from ARDS.</p><div style="margin:10px auto 10px auto; text-align:center; width:100%; overflow:hidden;">\r\n                        <div id="snack_dex8"></div>\r\n                      </div>\r\n                      <br>\n<p>Scientists administered a toxin to the mice that trigger the disease. One group were then given THC to see if it would block the strong immune response that leads to ARDS. After performing three studies, they found that all the animals who were not treated died after developing the disease, but those treated with THC \xe2\x80\x98led to 100 per cent survival\xe2\x80\x99.</p>\n<p>Although scientists said their research is not conclusive, they said THC showed promising results that it could potentially be used to treat complications caused by COVID-19.</p><div style="margin:10px auto 10px auto; text-align:center; width:100%; overflow:hidden;">\r\n                      <div id="snack_dex7"></div>\r\n                    </div>\r\n                    <br>\n<p>So it&#8217;s not exactly going to cure COVID-19 but it could help people recover and prevent the virus from becoming fatal.</p>\n<blockquote>\n<h3>Researchers insist they are not suggesting that people use marijuana to attempt to treat COVID-19 or help the symptoms.</h3>\n</blockquote>\n<p>One of the study\xe2\x80\x99s co-authors, Prakash Nagarkatti, explained: \xe2\x80\x98I just want to make sure our research is <strong>NOT</strong> interpreted as marijuana is good for COVID 19. \xe2\x80\x98If you start using THC early on it might worsen the effect because it suppresses the immune system.\xe2\x80\x99 The scientist explained that ARDS is triggered when the immune system \xe2\x80\x98goes haywire and starts destroying your lungs and all your other organs\xe2\x80\x99.</p>\n<p>Nagarkatti said: \xe2\x80\x98It\xe2\x80\x99s like a car where you\xe2\x80\x99re putting on a lot of accelerator, but the brakes aren\xe2\x80\x99t working. Basically what\xe2\x80\x99s going to happen is your car is going to crash because you can\xe2\x80\x99t stop it. And that\xe2\x80\x99s basically what\xe2\x80\x99s happening with ARDS.\xe2\x80\x99 Meanwhile, a study in Israel using a unique terpene formulation found in cannabis has shown early promising results for the treatment of viral infections, including COVID-19.</p>\n<p>Researchers found that using the terpene combination with CBD was twice as effective as Dexamethasone, which has been used in patients with severe complications caused by COVID-19.</p>\n<p>We hope you enjoyed this article \xe2\x80\x9cChemicals in cannabis are helping cure COVID-19\xe2\x80\x9d.</p>\n<p>Euro Weekly News is delighted to continue to be able to bring you a range of News that doesn\xe2\x80\x99t cost you anything but your internet connection. Whether it\xe2\x80\x99s Local Spanish News or International Entertainment News, we\xe2\x80\x99ve got you covered!</p>\n<!-- AddThis Advanced Settings above via filter on the_content --><!-- AddThis
